3507:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3508: }

3510: static PetscErrorCode MatMultTranspose_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, Vec xx, Vec yy)
3511: {
3512:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3513:   PetscCall(MatMultAddKernel_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(A, xx, NULL, yy, PETSC_TRUE, PETSC_FALSE));
3514:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3515: }

3517: __global__ static void ScatterAdd(PetscInt n, PetscInt *idx, const PetscScalar *x, PetscScalar *y)
3518: {
3519:   int i = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
3520:   if (i < n) y[idx[i]] += x[i];
3521: }

3523: /* z = op(A) x + y. If trans & !herm, op = ^T; if trans & herm, op = ^H; if !trans, op = no-op */
3524: static PetscErrorCode MatMultAddKernel_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, Vec xx, Vec yy, Vec zz, PetscBool trans, PetscBool herm)
3525: {
3526:   Mat_SeqAIJ                   *a              = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;
3527:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE           *cusparsestruct = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
3528:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *matstruct;
3529:   PetscScalar                  *xarray, *zarray, *dptr, *beta, *xptr;
3530:   cusparseOperation_t           opA = CUSPARSE_OPERATION_NON_TRANSPOSE;
3531:   PetscBool                     compressed;
3532: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3533:   PetscInt nx, ny;
3534: #endif

3536:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3537:   PetscCheck(!herm || trans, PetscObjectComm((PetscObject)A), PETSC_ERR_GPU, "Hermitian and not transpose not supported");
3538:   if (!a->nz) {
3539:     if (yy) PetscCall(VecSeq_CUDA::Copy(yy, zz));
3540:     else PetscCall(VecSeq_CUDA::Set(zz, 0));
3541:     PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3542:   }
3543:   /* The line below is necessary due to the operations that modify the matrix on the CPU (axpy, scale, etc) */
3544:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
3545:   if (!trans) {
3546:     matstruct = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *)cusparsestruct->mat;
3547:     PetscCheck(matstruct, PetscObjectComm((PetscObject)A), PETSC_ERR_GPU, "SeqAIJCUSPARSE does not have a 'mat' (need to fix)");
3548:   } else {
3549:     if (herm || !A->form_explicit_transpose) {
3550:       opA       = herm ? CUSPARSE_OPERATION_CONJUGATE_TRANSPOSE : CUSPARSE_OPERATION_TRANSPOSE;
3551:       matstruct = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *)cusparsestruct->mat;
3552:     } else {
3553:       if (!cusparsestruct->matTranspose) PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEFormExplicitTranspose(A));
3554:       matstruct = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *)cusparsestruct->matTranspose;
3555:     }
3556:   }
3557:   /* Does the matrix use compressed rows (i.e., drop zero rows)? */
3558:   compressed = matstruct->cprowIndices ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;

3560:   try {
3561:     PetscCall(VecCUDAGetArrayRead(xx, (const PetscScalar **)&xarray));
3562:     if (yy == zz) PetscCall(VecCUDAGetArray(zz, &zarray)); /* read & write zz, so need to get up-to-date zarray on GPU */
3563:     else PetscCall(VecCUDAGetArrayWrite(zz, &zarray));     /* write zz, so no need to init zarray on GPU */

3565:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
3566:     if (opA == CUSPARSE_OPERATION_NON_TRANSPOSE) {
3567:       /* z = A x + beta y.
3568:          If A is compressed (with less rows), then Ax is shorter than the full z, so we need a work vector to store Ax.
3569:          When A is non-compressed, and z = y, we can set beta=1 to compute y = Ax + y in one call.
3570:       */
3571:       xptr = xarray;
3572:       dptr = compressed ? cusparsestruct->workVector->data().get() : zarray;
3573:       beta = (yy == zz && !compressed) ? matstruct->beta_one : matstruct->beta_zero;
3574: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3575:       /* Get length of x, y for y=Ax. ny might be shorter than the work vector's allocated length, since the work vector is
3576:           allocated to accommodate different uses. So we get the length info directly from mat.
3577:        */
3578:       if (cusparsestruct->format == MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR) {
3579:         CsrMatrix *mat = (CsrMatrix *)matstruct->mat;
3580:         nx             = mat->num_cols;
3581:         ny             = mat->num_rows;
3582:       }
3583: #endif
3584:     } else {
3585:       /* z = A^T x + beta y
3586:          If A is compressed, then we need a work vector as the shorter version of x to compute A^T x.
3587:          Note A^Tx is of full length, so we set beta to 1.0 if y exists.
3588:        */
3589:       xptr = compressed ? cusparsestruct->workVector->data().get() : xarray;
3590:       dptr = zarray;
3591:       beta = yy ? matstruct->beta_one : matstruct->beta_zero;
3592:       if (compressed) { /* Scatter x to work vector */
3593:         thrust::device_ptr<PetscScalar> xarr = thrust::device_pointer_cast(xarray);

3595:         thrust::for_each(
3596: #if PetscDefined(HAVE_THRUST_ASYNC)
3597:           thrust::cuda::par.on(PetscDefaultCudaStream),
3598: #endif
3599:           thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(cusparsestruct->workVector->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(xarr, matstruct->cprowIndices->begin()))),
3600:           thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(cusparsestruct->workVector->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(xarr, matstruct->cprowIndices->begin()))) + matstruct->cprowIndices->size(), VecCUDAEqualsReverse());
3601:       }
3602: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3603:       if (cusparsestruct->format == MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR) {
3604:         CsrMatrix *mat = (CsrMatrix *)matstruct->mat;
3605:         nx             = mat->num_rows;
3606:         ny             = mat->num_cols;
3607:       }
3608: #endif
3609:     }

3611:     /* csr_spmv does y = alpha op(A) x + beta y */
3612:     if (cusparsestruct->format == MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR) {
3613: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3614:       PetscCheck(opA >= 0 && opA <= 2, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "cuSPARSE ABI on cusparseOperation_t has changed and PETSc has not been updated accordingly");
3615:       if (!matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].initialized) { /* built on demand */
3616:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseCreateDnVec(&matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecXDescr, nx, xptr, cusparse_scalartype));
3617:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseCreateDnVec(&matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecYDescr, ny, dptr, cusparse_scalartype));
3618:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(
3619:           cusparseSpMV_bufferSize(cusparsestruct->handle, opA, matstruct->alpha_one, matstruct->matDescr, matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecXDescr, beta, matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecYDescr, cusparse_scalartype, cusparsestruct->spmvAlg, &matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].spmvBufferSize));
3620:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc(&matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].spmvBuffer, matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].spmvBufferSize));

3622:         matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].initialized = PETSC_TRUE;
3623:       } else {
3624:         /* x, y's value pointers might change between calls, but their shape is kept, so we just update pointers */
3625:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDnVecSetValues(matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecXDescr, xptr));
3626:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDnVecSetValues(matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecYDescr, dptr));
3627:       }

3629:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSpMV(cusparsestruct->handle, opA, matstruct->alpha_one, matstruct->matDescr, /* built in MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU() or MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEFormExplicitTranspose() */
3630:                                      matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecXDescr, beta, matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].vecYDescr, cusparse_scalartype, cusparsestruct->spmvAlg, matstruct->cuSpMV[opA].spmvBuffer));
3631: #else
3632:       CsrMatrix *mat = (CsrMatrix *)matstruct->mat;
3633:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparse_csr_spmv(cusparsestruct->handle, opA, mat->num_rows, mat->num_cols, mat->num_entries, matstruct->alpha_one, matstruct->descr, mat->values->data().get(), mat->row_offsets->data().get(), mat->column_indices->data().get(), xptr, beta, dptr));
3634: #endif
3635:     } else {
3636:       if (cusparsestruct->nrows) {
3637: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3638:         SETERRQ(PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL and MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB are not supported since CUDA-11.0");
3639: #else
3640:         cusparseHybMat_t hybMat = (cusparseHybMat_t)matstruct->mat;
3641:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparse_hyb_spmv(cusparsestruct->handle, opA, matstruct->alpha_one, matstruct->descr, hybMat, xptr, beta, dptr));
3642: #endif
3643:       }
3644:     }
3645:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());

3647:     if (opA == CUSPARSE_OPERATION_NON_TRANSPOSE) {
3648:       if (yy) {                                      /* MatMultAdd: zz = A*xx + yy */
3649:         if (compressed) {                            /* A is compressed. We first copy yy to zz, then ScatterAdd the work vector to zz */
3650:           PetscCall(VecSeq_CUDA::Copy(yy, zz));      /* zz = yy */
3651:         } else if (zz != yy) {                       /* A is not compressed. zz already contains A*xx, and we just need to add yy */
3652:           PetscCall(VecSeq_CUDA::AXPY(zz, 1.0, yy)); /* zz += yy */
3653:         }
3654:       } else if (compressed) { /* MatMult: zz = A*xx. A is compressed, so we zero zz first, then ScatterAdd the work vector to zz */
3655:         PetscCall(VecSeq_CUDA::Set(zz, 0));
3656:       }

3658:       /* ScatterAdd the result from work vector into the full vector when A is compressed */
3659:       if (compressed) {
3660:         PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
3661:         /* I wanted to make this for_each asynchronous but failed. thrust::async::for_each() returns an event (internally registered)
3662:            and in the destructor of the scope, it will call cudaStreamSynchronize() on this stream. One has to store all events to
3663:            prevent that. So I just add a ScatterAdd kernel.
3664:          */
3665: #if 0
3666:         thrust::device_ptr<PetscScalar> zptr = thrust::device_pointer_cast(zarray);
3667:         thrust::async::for_each(thrust::cuda::par.on(cusparsestruct->stream),
3668:                          thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(cusparsestruct->workVector->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(zptr, matstruct->cprowIndices->begin()))),
3669:                          thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(cusparsestruct->workVector->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(zptr, matstruct->cprowIndices->begin()))) + matstruct->cprowIndices->size(),
3670:                          VecCUDAPlusEquals());
3671: #else
3672:         PetscInt n = matstruct->cprowIndices->size();
3673:         ScatterAdd<<<(n + 255) / 256, 256, 0, PetscDefaultCudaStream>>>(n, matstruct->cprowIndices->data().get(), cusparsestruct->workVector->data().get(), zarray);
3674: #endif
3675:         PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
3676:       }
3677:     } else {
3678:       if (yy && yy != zz) PetscCall(VecSeq_CUDA::AXPY(zz, 1.0, yy)); /* zz += yy */
3679:     }
3680:     PetscCall(VecCUDARestoreArrayRead(xx, (const PetscScalar **)&xarray));
3681:     if (yy == zz) PetscCall(VecCUDARestoreArray(zz, &zarray));
3682:     else PetscCall(VecCUDARestoreArrayWrite(zz, &zarray));
3683:   } catch (char *ex) {
3684:     SETERRQ(PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_LIB, "CUSPARSE error: %s", ex);
3685:   }
3686:   if (yy) {
3687:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuFlops(2.0 * a->nz));
3688:   } else {
3689:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuFlops(2.0 * a->nz - a->nonzerorowcnt));
3690:   }
3691:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3692: }

3694: static PetscErrorCode MatMultTransposeAdd_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, Vec xx, Vec yy, Vec zz)
3695: {
3696:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3697:   PetscCall(MatMultAddKernel_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(A, xx, yy, zz, PETSC_TRUE, PETSC_FALSE));
3698:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3699: }

3701: static PetscErrorCode MatAssemblyEnd_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, MatAssemblyType mode)
3702: {
3703:   PetscObjectState    onnz = A->nonzerostate;
3704:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;

3706:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3707:   PetscCall(MatAssemblyEnd_SeqAIJ(A, mode));
3708:   if (onnz != A->nonzerostate && cusp->deviceMat) {
3709:     PetscCall(PetscInfo(A, "Destroy device mat since nonzerostate changed\n"));
3710:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(cusp->deviceMat));
3711:     cusp->deviceMat = NULL;
3712:   }
3713:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3714: }

3716: /*@
3717:    MatCreateSeqAIJCUSPARSE - Creates a sparse matrix in `MATAIJCUSPARSE` (compressed row) format
3718:    (the default parallel PETSc format). This matrix will ultimately pushed down
3719:    to NVIDIA GPUs and use the CuSPARSE library for calculations. For good matrix
3720:    assembly performance the user should preallocate the matrix storage by setting
3721:    the parameter `nz` (or the array `nnz`).

3723:    Collective

3725:    Input Parameters:
3726: +  comm - MPI communicator, set to `PETSC_COMM_SELF`
3727: .  m - number of rows
3728: .  n - number of columns
3729: .  nz - number of nonzeros per row (same for all rows), ignored if `nnz` is provide
3730: -  nnz - array containing the number of nonzeros in the various rows (possibly different for each row) or `NULL`

3732:    Output Parameter:
3733: .  A - the matrix

3735:    Level: intermediate

3737:    Notes:
3738:    It is recommended that one use the `MatCreate()`, `MatSetType()` and/or `MatSetFromOptions()`,
3739:    MatXXXXSetPreallocation() paradgm instead of this routine directly.
3740:    [MatXXXXSetPreallocation() is, for example, `MatSeqAIJSetPreallocation()`]

3742:    The AIJ format, also called
3743:    compressed row storage, is fully compatible with standard Fortran
3744:    storage.  That is, the stored row and column indices can begin at
3745:    either one (as in Fortran) or zero.

3747:    Specify the preallocated storage with either nz or nnz (not both).
3748:    Set `nz` = `PETSC_DEFAULT` and `nnz` = `NULL` for PETSc to control dynamic memory
3749:    allocation.

3751: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE`, `MatCreate()`, `MatCreateAIJ()`, `MatSetValues()`, `MatSeqAIJSetColumnIndices()`, `MatCreateSeqAIJWithArrays()`, `MatCreateAIJ()`, `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE`, `MATAIJCUSPARSE`
3752: @*/
3753: PetscErrorCode MatCreateSeqAIJCUSPARSE(MPI_Comm comm, PetscInt m, PetscInt n, PetscInt nz, const PetscInt nnz[], Mat *A)
3754: {
3755:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3756:   PetscCall(MatCreate(comm, A));
3757:   PetscCall(MatSetSizes(*A, m, n, m, n));
3758:   PetscCall(MatSetType(*A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE));
3759:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJSetPreallocation_SeqAIJ(*A, nz, (PetscInt *)nnz));
3760:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3761: }

3763: static PetscErrorCode MatDestroy_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A)
3764: {
3765:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3766:   if (A->factortype == MAT_FACTOR_NONE) {
3767:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSE_Destroy((Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE **)&A->spptr));
3768:   } else {
3769:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors_Destroy((Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors **)&A->spptr));
3770:   }
3771:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSeqAIJCopySubArray_C", NULL));
3772:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatCUSPARSESetFormat_C", NULL));
3773:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatCUSPARSESetUseCPUSolve_C", NULL));
3774:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqdensecuda_C", NULL));
3775:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqdense_C", NULL));
3776:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqaijcusparse_C", NULL));
3777:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatFactorGetSolverType_C", NULL));
3778:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSetPreallocationCOO_C", NULL));
3779:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSetValuesCOO_C", NULL));
3780:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatConvert_seqaijcusparse_hypre_C", NULL));
3781:   PetscCall(MatDestroy_SeqAIJ(A));
3782:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3783: }

3785: PETSC_INTERN PetscErrorCode MatConvert_SeqAIJ_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat, MatType, MatReuse, Mat *);
3786: static PetscErrorCode       MatBindToCPU_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat, PetscBool);
3787: static PetscErrorCode       MatDuplicate_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, MatDuplicateOption cpvalues, Mat *B)
3788: {
3789:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3790:   PetscCall(MatDuplicate_SeqAIJ(A, cpvalues, B));
3791:   PetscCall(MatConvert_SeqAIJ_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(*B, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE, MAT_INPLACE_MATRIX, B));
3792:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3793: }

3795: static PetscErrorCode MatAXPY_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat Y, PetscScalar a, Mat X, MatStructure str)
3796: {
3797:   Mat_SeqAIJ         *x = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)X->data, *y = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)Y->data;
3798:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cy;
3799:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cx;
3800:   PetscScalar        *ay;
3801:   const PetscScalar  *ax;
3802:   CsrMatrix          *csry, *csrx;

3804:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3805:   cy = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)Y->spptr;
3806:   cx = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)X->spptr;
3807:   if (X->ops->axpy != Y->ops->axpy) {
3808:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(Y, PETSC_FALSE));
3809:     PetscCall(MatAXPY_SeqAIJ(Y, a, X, str));
3810:     PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3811:   }
3812:   /* if we are here, it means both matrices are bound to GPU */
3813:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(Y));
3814:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(X));
3815:   PetscCheck(cy->format == MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR, PetscObjectComm((PetscObject)Y), PETSC_ERR_GPU, "only MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR supported");
3816:   PetscCheck(cx->format == MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR, PetscObjectComm((PetscObject)X), PETSC_ERR_GPU, "only MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR supported");
3817:   csry = (CsrMatrix *)cy->mat->mat;
3818:   csrx = (CsrMatrix *)cx->mat->mat;
3819:   /* see if we can turn this into a cublas axpy */
3820:   if (str != SAME_NONZERO_PATTERN && x->nz == y->nz && !x->compressedrow.use && !y->compressedrow.use) {
3821:     bool eq = thrust::equal(thrust::device, csry->row_offsets->begin(), csry->row_offsets->end(), csrx->row_offsets->begin());
3822:     if (eq) eq = thrust::equal(thrust::device, csry->column_indices->begin(), csry->column_indices->end(), csrx->column_indices->begin());
3823:     if (eq) str = SAME_NONZERO_PATTERN;
3824:   }
3825:   /* spgeam is buggy with one column */
3826:   if (Y->cmap->n == 1 && str != SAME_NONZERO_PATTERN) str = DIFFERENT_NONZERO_PATTERN;

3828:   if (str == SUBSET_NONZERO_PATTERN) {
3829:     PetscScalar b = 1.0;
3830: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3831:     size_t bufferSize;
3832:     void  *buffer;
3833: #endif

3835:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead(X, &ax));
3836:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray(Y, &ay));
3837:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetPointerMode(cy->handle, CUSPARSE_POINTER_MODE_HOST));
3838: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
3839:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparse_csr_spgeam_bufferSize(cy->handle, Y->rmap->n, Y->cmap->n, &a, cx->mat->descr, x->nz, ax, csrx->row_offsets->data().get(), csrx->column_indices->data().get(), &b, cy->mat->descr, y->nz, ay, csry->row_offsets->data().get(),
3840:                                                      csry->column_indices->data().get(), cy->mat->descr, ay, csry->row_offsets->data().get(), csry->column_indices->data().get(), &bufferSize));
3841:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc(&buffer, bufferSize));
3842:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
3843:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparse_csr_spgeam(cy->handle, Y->rmap->n, Y->cmap->n, &a, cx->mat->descr, x->nz, ax, csrx->row_offsets->data().get(), csrx->column_indices->data().get(), &b, cy->mat->descr, y->nz, ay, csry->row_offsets->data().get(),
3844:                                           csry->column_indices->data().get(), cy->mat->descr, ay, csry->row_offsets->data().get(), csry->column_indices->data().get(), buffer));
3845:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuFlops(x->nz + y->nz));
3846:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
3847:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(buffer));
3848: #else
3849:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
3850:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparse_csr_spgeam(cy->handle, Y->rmap->n, Y->cmap->n, &a, cx->mat->descr, x->nz, ax, csrx->row_offsets->data().get(), csrx->column_indices->data().get(), &b, cy->mat->descr, y->nz, ay, csry->row_offsets->data().get(),
3851:                                           csry->column_indices->data().get(), cy->mat->descr, ay, csry->row_offsets->data().get(), csry->column_indices->data().get()));
3852:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuFlops(x->nz + y->nz));
3853:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
3854: #endif
3855:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetPointerMode(cy->handle, CUSPARSE_POINTER_MODE_DEVICE));
3856:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayRead(X, &ax));
3857:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray(Y, &ay));
3858:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJInvalidateDiagonal(Y));
3859:   } else if (str == SAME_NONZERO_PATTERN) {
3860:     cublasHandle_t cublasv2handle;
3861:     PetscBLASInt   one = 1, bnz = 1;

3863:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead(X, &ax));
3864:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray(Y, &ay));
3865:     PetscCall(PetscCUBLASGetHandle(&cublasv2handle));
3866:     PetscCall(PetscBLASIntCast(x->nz, &bnz));
3867:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
3868:     PetscCallCUBLAS(cublasXaxpy(cublasv2handle, bnz, &a, ax, one, ay, one));
3869:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuFlops(2.0 * bnz));
3870:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
3871:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayRead(X, &ax));
3872:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray(Y, &ay));
3873:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJInvalidateDiagonal(Y));
3874:   } else {
3875:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(Y, PETSC_FALSE));
3876:     PetscCall(MatAXPY_SeqAIJ(Y, a, X, str));
3877:   }
3878:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3879: }

3881: static PetscErrorCode MatScale_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat Y, PetscScalar a)
3882: {
3883:   Mat_SeqAIJ    *y = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)Y->data;
3884:   PetscScalar   *ay;
3885:   cublasHandle_t cublasv2handle;
3886:   PetscBLASInt   one = 1, bnz = 1;

3888:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3889:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray(Y, &ay));
3890:   PetscCall(PetscCUBLASGetHandle(&cublasv2handle));
3891:   PetscCall(PetscBLASIntCast(y->nz, &bnz));
3892:   PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
3893:   PetscCallCUBLAS(cublasXscal(cublasv2handle, bnz, &a, ay, one));
3894:   PetscCall(PetscLogGpuFlops(bnz));
3895:   PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
3896:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray(Y, &ay));
3897:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJInvalidateDiagonal(Y));
3898:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3899: }

3901: static PetscErrorCode MatZeroEntries_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A)
3902: {
3903:   PetscBool   both = PETSC_FALSE;
3904:   Mat_SeqAIJ *a    = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;

3906:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3907:   if (A->factortype == MAT_FACTOR_NONE) {
3908:     Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *spptr = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
3909:     if (spptr->mat) {
3910:       CsrMatrix *matrix = (CsrMatrix *)spptr->mat->mat;
3911:       if (matrix->values) {
3912:         both = PETSC_TRUE;
3913:         thrust::fill(thrust::device, matrix->values->begin(), matrix->values->end(), 0.);
3914:       }
3915:     }
3916:     if (spptr->matTranspose) {
3917:       CsrMatrix *matrix = (CsrMatrix *)spptr->matTranspose->mat;
3918:       if (matrix->values) thrust::fill(thrust::device, matrix->values->begin(), matrix->values->end(), 0.);
3919:     }
3920:   }
3921:   PetscCall(PetscArrayzero(a->a, a->i[A->rmap->n]));
3922:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJInvalidateDiagonal(A));
3923:   if (both) A->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_BOTH;
3924:   else A->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_CPU;
3925:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3926: }

3928: static PetscErrorCode MatBindToCPU_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, PetscBool flg)
3929: {
3930:   Mat_SeqAIJ *a = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;

3932:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3933:   if (A->factortype != MAT_FACTOR_NONE) {
3934:     A->boundtocpu = flg;
3935:     PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3936:   }
3937:   if (flg) {
3938:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyFromGPU(A));

3940:     A->ops->scale                     = MatScale_SeqAIJ;
3941:     A->ops->axpy                      = MatAXPY_SeqAIJ;
3942:     A->ops->zeroentries               = MatZeroEntries_SeqAIJ;
3943:     A->ops->mult                      = MatMult_SeqAIJ;
3944:     A->ops->multadd                   = MatMultAdd_SeqAIJ;
3945:     A->ops->multtranspose             = MatMultTranspose_SeqAIJ;
3946:     A->ops->multtransposeadd          = MatMultTransposeAdd_SeqAIJ;
3947:     A->ops->multhermitiantranspose    = NULL;
3948:     A->ops->multhermitiantransposeadd = NULL;
3949:     A->ops->productsetfromoptions     = MatProductSetFromOptions_SeqAIJ;
3950:     PetscCall(PetscMemzero(a->ops, sizeof(Mat_SeqAIJOps)));
3951:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSeqAIJCopySubArray_C", NULL));
3952:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqdensecuda_C", NULL));
3953:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqdense_C", NULL));
3954:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSetPreallocationCOO_C", NULL));
3955:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSetValuesCOO_C", NULL));
3956:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqaijcusparse_C", NULL));
3957:   } else {
3958:     A->ops->scale                     = MatScale_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3959:     A->ops->axpy                      = MatAXPY_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3960:     A->ops->zeroentries               = MatZeroEntries_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3961:     A->ops->mult                      = MatMult_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3962:     A->ops->multadd                   = MatMultAdd_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3963:     A->ops->multtranspose             = MatMultTranspose_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3964:     A->ops->multtransposeadd          = MatMultTransposeAdd_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3965:     A->ops->multhermitiantranspose    = MatMultHermitianTranspose_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3966:     A->ops->multhermitiantransposeadd = MatMultHermitianTransposeAdd_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3967:     A->ops->productsetfromoptions     = MatProductSetFromOptions_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3968:     a->ops->getarray                  = MatSeqAIJGetArray_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3969:     a->ops->restorearray              = MatSeqAIJRestoreArray_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3970:     a->ops->getarrayread              = MatSeqAIJGetArrayRead_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3971:     a->ops->restorearrayread          = MatSeqAIJRestoreArrayRead_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3972:     a->ops->getarraywrite             = MatSeqAIJGetArrayWrite_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3973:     a->ops->restorearraywrite         = MatSeqAIJRestoreArrayWrite_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
3974:     a->ops->getcsrandmemtype          = MatSeqAIJGetCSRAndMemType_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;

3976:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSeqAIJCopySubArray_C", MatSeqAIJCopySubArray_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
3977:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqdensecuda_C", MatProductSetFromOptions_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
3978:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqdense_C", MatProductSetFromOptions_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
3979:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSetPreallocationCOO_C", MatSetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
3980:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatSetValuesCOO_C", MatSetValuesCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
3981:     PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)A, "MatProductSetFromOptions_seqaijcusparse_seqaijcusparse_C", MatProductSetFromOptions_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
3982:   }
3983:   A->boundtocpu = flg;
3984:   if (flg && a->inode.size) {
3985:     a->inode.use = PETSC_TRUE;
3986:   } else {
3987:     a->inode.use = PETSC_FALSE;
3988:   }
3989:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
3990: }

3992: PETSC_INTERN PetscErrorCode MatConvert_SeqAIJ_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, MatType, MatReuse reuse, Mat *newmat)
3993: {
3994:   Mat B;

3996:   PetscFunctionBegin;
3997:   PetscCall(PetscDeviceInitialize(PETSC_DEVICE_CUDA)); /* first use of CUSPARSE may be via MatConvert */
3998:   if (reuse == MAT_INITIAL_MATRIX) {
3999:     PetscCall(MatDuplicate(A, MAT_COPY_VALUES, newmat));
4000:   } else if (reuse == MAT_REUSE_MATRIX) {
4001:     PetscCall(MatCopy(A, *newmat, SAME_NONZERO_PATTERN));
4002:   }
4003:   B = *newmat;

4005:   PetscCall(PetscFree(B->defaultvectype));
4006:   PetscCall(PetscStrallocpy(VECCUDA, &B->defaultvectype));

4008:   if (reuse != MAT_REUSE_MATRIX && !B->spptr) {
4009:     if (B->factortype == MAT_FACTOR_NONE) {
4010:       Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *spptr;
4011:       PetscCall(PetscNew(&spptr));
4012:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseCreate(&spptr->handle));
4013:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetStream(spptr->handle, PetscDefaultCudaStream));
4014:       spptr->format = MAT_CUSPARSE_CSR;
4015: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
4016:   #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 4, 0)
4017:       spptr->spmvAlg = CUSPARSE_SPMV_CSR_ALG1; /* default, since we only support csr */
4018:   #else
4019:       spptr->spmvAlg = CUSPARSE_CSRMV_ALG1; /* default, since we only support csr */
4020:   #endif
4021:       spptr->spmmAlg    = CUSPARSE_SPMM_CSR_ALG1; /* default, only support column-major dense matrix B */
4022:       spptr->csr2cscAlg = CUSPARSE_CSR2CSC_ALG1;
4023: #endif
4024:       B->spptr = spptr;
4025:     } else {
4026:       Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors *spptr;

4028:       PetscCall(PetscNew(&spptr));
4029:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseCreate(&spptr->handle));
4030:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetStream(spptr->handle, PetscDefaultCudaStream));
4031:       B->spptr = spptr;
4032:     }
4033:     B->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_UNALLOCATED;
4034:   }
4035:   B->ops->assemblyend    = MatAssemblyEnd_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
4036:   B->ops->destroy        = MatDestroy_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
4037:   B->ops->setoption      = MatSetOption_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
4038:   B->ops->setfromoptions = MatSetFromOptions_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
4039:   B->ops->bindtocpu      = MatBindToCPU_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;
4040:   B->ops->duplicate      = MatDuplicate_SeqAIJCUSPARSE;

4042:   PetscCall(MatBindToCPU_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(B, PETSC_FALSE));
4043:   PetscCall(PetscObjectChangeTypeName((PetscObject)B, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE));
4044:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)B, "MatCUSPARSESetFormat_C", MatCUSPARSESetFormat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
4045: #if defined(PETSC_HAVE_HYPRE)
4046:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)B, "MatConvert_seqaijcusparse_hypre_C", MatConvert_AIJ_HYPRE));
4047: #endif
4048:   PetscCall(PetscObjectComposeFunction((PetscObject)B, "MatCUSPARSESetUseCPUSolve_C", MatCUSPARSESetUseCPUSolve_SeqAIJCUSPARSE));
4049:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4050: }

4052: PETSC_EXTERN PetscErrorCode MatCreate_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat B)
4053: {
4054:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4055:   PetscCall(MatCreate_SeqAIJ(B));
4056:   PetscCall(MatConvert_SeqAIJ_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(B, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE, MAT_INPLACE_MATRIX, &B));
4057:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4058: }

4060: /*MC
4061:    MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE - MATAIJCUSPARSE = "(seq)aijcusparse" - A matrix type to be used for sparse matrices.

4063:    A matrix type type whose data resides on NVIDIA GPUs. These matrices can be in either
4064:    CSR, ELL, or Hybrid format.
4065:    All matrix calculations are performed on NVIDIA GPUs using the CuSPARSE library.

4067:    Options Database Keys:
4068: +  -mat_type aijcusparse - sets the matrix type to "seqaijcusparse" during a call to `MatSetFromOptions()`
4069: .  -mat_cusparse_storage_format csr - sets the storage format of matrices (for `MatMult()` and factors in `MatSolve()`).
4070:                                       Other options include ell (ellpack) or hyb (hybrid).
4071: .  -mat_cusparse_mult_storage_format csr - sets the storage format of matrices (for `MatMult()`). Other options include ell (ellpack) or hyb (hybrid).
4072: -  -mat_cusparse_use_cpu_solve - Do `MatSolve()` on CPU

4074:   Level: beginner

4076: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatCreateSeqAIJCUSPARSE()`, `MatCUSPARSESetUseCPUSolve()`, `MATAIJCUSPARSE`, `MatCreateAIJCUSPARSE()`, `MatCUSPARSESetFormat()`, `MatCUSPARSEStorageFormat`, `MatCUSPARSEFormatOperation`
4077: M*/

4079: PETSC_EXTERN PetscErrorCode MatGetFactor_seqaijcusparse_cusparse_band(Mat, MatFactorType, Mat *);

4081: PETSC_EXTERN PetscErrorCode MatSolverTypeRegister_CUSPARSE(void)
4082: {
4083:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4084:   PetscCall(MatSolverTypeRegister(MATSOLVERCUSPARSEBAND, MATSEQAIJ, MAT_FACTOR_LU, MatGetFactor_seqaijcusparse_cusparse_band));
4085:   PetscCall(MatSolverTypeRegister(MATSOLVERCUSPARSE, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE, MAT_FACTOR_LU, MatGetFactor_seqaijcusparse_cusparse));
4086:   PetscCall(MatSolverTypeRegister(MATSOLVERCUSPARSE, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE, MAT_FACTOR_CHOLESKY, MatGetFactor_seqaijcusparse_cusparse));
4087:   PetscCall(MatSolverTypeRegister(MATSOLVERCUSPARSE, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE, MAT_FACTOR_ILU, MatGetFactor_seqaijcusparse_cusparse));
4088:   PetscCall(MatSolverTypeRegister(MATSOLVERCUSPARSE, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE, MAT_FACTOR_ICC, MatGetFactor_seqaijcusparse_cusparse));

4090:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4091: }

4093: static PetscErrorCode MatResetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat mat)
4094: {
4095:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)mat->spptr;

4097:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4098:   if (!cusp) PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4099:   delete cusp->cooPerm;
4100:   delete cusp->cooPerm_a;
4101:   cusp->cooPerm   = NULL;
4102:   cusp->cooPerm_a = NULL;
4103:   if (cusp->use_extended_coo) {
4104:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(cusp->jmap_d));
4105:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(cusp->perm_d));
4106:   }
4107:   cusp->use_extended_coo = PETSC_FALSE;
4108:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4109: }

4111: static PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSE_Destroy(Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE **cusparsestruct)
4112: {
4113:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4114:   if (*cusparsestruct) {
4115:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&(*cusparsestruct)->mat, (*cusparsestruct)->format));
4116:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&(*cusparsestruct)->matTranspose, (*cusparsestruct)->format));
4117:     delete (*cusparsestruct)->workVector;
4118:     delete (*cusparsestruct)->rowoffsets_gpu;
4119:     delete (*cusparsestruct)->cooPerm;
4120:     delete (*cusparsestruct)->cooPerm_a;
4121:     delete (*cusparsestruct)->csr2csc_i;
4122:     if ((*cusparsestruct)->handle) PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroy((*cusparsestruct)->handle));
4123:     if ((*cusparsestruct)->jmap_d) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*cusparsestruct)->jmap_d));
4124:     if ((*cusparsestruct)->perm_d) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*cusparsestruct)->perm_d));
4125:     PetscCall(PetscFree(*cusparsestruct));
4126:   }
4127:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4128: }

4130: static PetscErrorCode CsrMatrix_Destroy(CsrMatrix **mat)
4131: {
4132:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4133:   if (*mat) {
4134:     delete (*mat)->values;
4135:     delete (*mat)->column_indices;
4136:     delete (*mat)->row_offsets;
4137:     delete *mat;
4138:     *mat = 0;
4139:   }
4140:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4141: }

4143: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_LT(11, 4, 0)
4144: static PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactorStruct **trifactor)
4145: {
4146:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4147:   if (*trifactor) {
4148:     if ((*trifactor)->descr) PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyMatDescr((*trifactor)->descr));
4149:     if ((*trifactor)->solveInfo) PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyCsrsvInfo((*trifactor)->solveInfo));
4150:     PetscCall(CsrMatrix_Destroy(&(*trifactor)->csrMat));
4151:     if ((*trifactor)->solveBuffer) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*trifactor)->solveBuffer));
4152:     if ((*trifactor)->AA_h) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFreeHost((*trifactor)->AA_h));
4153:   #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
4154:     if ((*trifactor)->csr2cscBuffer) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*trifactor)->csr2cscBuffer));
4155:   #endif
4156:     PetscCall(PetscFree(*trifactor));
4157:   }

4159: }
4160: #endif

4162: static PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct **matstruct, MatCUSPARSEStorageFormat format)
4163: {
4164:   CsrMatrix *mat;

4166:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4167:   if (*matstruct) {
4168:     if ((*matstruct)->mat) {
4169:       if (format == MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL || format == MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB) {
4170: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
4171:         SETERRQ(PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL and MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB are not supported since CUDA-11.0");
4172: #else
4173:         cusparseHybMat_t hybMat = (cusparseHybMat_t)(*matstruct)->mat;
4174:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyHybMat(hybMat));
4175: #endif
4176:       } else {
4177:         mat = (CsrMatrix *)(*matstruct)->mat;
4178:         PetscCall(CsrMatrix_Destroy(&mat));
4179:       }
4180:     }
4181:     if ((*matstruct)->descr) PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyMatDescr((*matstruct)->descr));
4182:     delete (*matstruct)->cprowIndices;
4183:     if ((*matstruct)->alpha_one) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*matstruct)->alpha_one));
4184:     if ((*matstruct)->beta_zero) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*matstruct)->beta_zero));
4185:     if ((*matstruct)->beta_one) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((*matstruct)->beta_one));

4187: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
4188:     Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *mdata = *matstruct;
4189:     if (mdata->matDescr) PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroySpMat(mdata->matDescr));
4190:     for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
4191:       if (mdata->cuSpMV[i].initialized) {
4192:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(mdata->cuSpMV[i].spmvBuffer));
4193:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyDnVec(mdata->cuSpMV[i].vecXDescr));
4194:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyDnVec(mdata->cuSpMV[i].vecYDescr));
4195:       }
4196:     }
4197: #endif
4198:     delete *matstruct;
4199:     *matstruct = NULL;
4200:   }
4201:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4202: }

4204: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors_Reset(Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors_p *trifactors)
4205: {
4206:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors *fs = *trifactors;

4208:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4209:   if (fs) {
4210: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_LT(11, 4, 0)
4211:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&fs->loTriFactorPtr));
4212:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&fs->upTriFactorPtr));
4213:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&fs->loTriFactorPtrTranspose));
4214:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&fs->upTriFactorPtrTranspose));
4215:     delete fs->workVector;
4216:     fs->workVector = NULL;
4217: #endif
4218:     delete fs->rpermIndices;
4219:     delete fs->cpermIndices;
4220:     fs->rpermIndices = NULL;
4221:     fs->cpermIndices = NULL;
4222:     if (fs->a_band_d) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->a_band_d));
4223:     if (fs->i_band_d) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->i_band_d));
4224:     fs->init_dev_prop = PETSC_FALSE;
4225: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 4, 0)
4226:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->csrRowPtr));
4227:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->csrColIdx));
4228:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->csrRowPtr32));

4231:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->diag));
4232:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->X));
4233:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(fs->Y));

4240:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroySpMat(fs->spMatDescr_L));
4241:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroySpMat(fs->spMatDescr_U));
4242:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSpSV_destroyDescr(fs->spsvDescr_L));
4243:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSpSV_destroyDescr(fs->spsvDescr_Lt));
4244:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSpSV_destroyDescr(fs->spsvDescr_U));
4245:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSpSV_destroyDescr(fs->spsvDescr_Ut));
4246:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyDnVec(fs->dnVecDescr_X));
4247:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyDnVec(fs->dnVecDescr_Y));
4248:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyCsrilu02Info(fs->ilu0Info_M));
4249:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroyCsric02Info(fs->ic0Info_M));
4250:     PetscCall(PetscFree(fs->csrRowPtr_h));
