4253:     fs->createdTransposeSpSVDescr    = PETSC_FALSE;
4254:     fs->updatedTransposeSpSVAnalysis = PETSC_FALSE;
4255: #endif
4256:   }
4257:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4258: }

4260: static PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors_Destroy(Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors **trifactors)
4261: {
4262:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4263:   if (*trifactors) {
4264:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSETriFactors_Reset(trifactors));
4265:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseDestroy((*trifactors)->handle));
4266:     PetscCall(PetscFree(*trifactors));
4267:   }
4268:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4269: }

4271: struct IJCompare {
4272:   __host__ __device__ inline bool operator()(const thrust::tuple<PetscInt, PetscInt> &t1, const thrust::tuple<PetscInt, PetscInt> &t2)
4273:   {
4274:     if (t1.get<0>() < t2.get<0>()) return true;
4275:     if (t1.get<0>() == t2.get<0>()) return t1.get<1>() < t2.get<1>();
4276:     return false;
4277:   }
4278: };

4280: struct IJEqual {
4281:   __host__ __device__ inline bool operator()(const thrust::tuple<PetscInt, PetscInt> &t1, const thrust::tuple<PetscInt, PetscInt> &t2)
4282:   {
4283:     if (t1.get<0>() != t2.get<0>() || t1.get<1>() != t2.get<1>()) return false;
4284:     return true;
4285:   }
4286: };

4288: struct IJDiff {
4289:   __host__ __device__ inline PetscInt operator()(const PetscInt &t1, const PetscInt &t2) { return t1 == t2 ? 0 : 1; }
4290: };

4292: struct IJSum {
4293:   __host__ __device__ inline PetscInt operator()(const PetscInt &t1, const PetscInt &t2) { return t1 || t2; }
4294: };

4296: #include <thrust/iterator/discard_iterator.h>
4297: /* Associated with MatSetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE_Basic() */
4298: PetscErrorCode MatSetValuesCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE_Basic(Mat A, const PetscScalar v[], InsertMode imode)
4299: {
4300:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE                   *cusp      = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4301:   Mat_SeqAIJ                           *a         = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;
4302:   THRUSTARRAY                          *cooPerm_v = NULL;
4303:   thrust::device_ptr<const PetscScalar> d_v;
4304:   CsrMatrix                            *matrix;
4305:   PetscInt                              n;

4307:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4308:   PetscCheck(cusp, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing CUSPARSE struct");
4309:   PetscCheck(cusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing CUSPARSE CsrMatrix");
4310:   if (!cusp->cooPerm) {
4311:     PetscCall(MatAssemblyBegin(A, MAT_FINAL_ASSEMBLY));
4312:     PetscCall(MatAssemblyEnd(A, MAT_FINAL_ASSEMBLY));
4313:     PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4314:   }
4315:   matrix = (CsrMatrix *)cusp->mat->mat;
4316:   PetscCheck(matrix->values, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing CUDA memory");
4317:   if (!v) {
4318:     if (imode == INSERT_VALUES) thrust::fill(thrust::device, matrix->values->begin(), matrix->values->end(), 0.);
4319:     goto finalize;
4320:   }
4321:   n = cusp->cooPerm->size();
4322:   if (isCudaMem(v)) {
4323:     d_v = thrust::device_pointer_cast(v);
4324:   } else {
4325:     cooPerm_v = new THRUSTARRAY(n);
4326:     cooPerm_v->assign(v, v + n);
4327:     d_v = cooPerm_v->data();
4328:     PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(n * sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4329:   }
4330:   PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
4331:   if (imode == ADD_VALUES) { /* ADD VALUES means add to existing ones */
4332:     if (cusp->cooPerm_a) {   /* there are repeated entries in d_v[], and we need to add these them */
4333:       THRUSTARRAY *cooPerm_w = new THRUSTARRAY(matrix->values->size());
4334:       auto         vbit      = thrust::make_permutation_iterator(d_v, cusp->cooPerm->begin());
4335:       /* thrust::reduce_by_key(keys_first,keys_last,values_first,keys_output,values_output)
4336:         cooPerm_a = [0,0,1,2,3,4]. The length is n, number of nonozeros in d_v[].
4337:         cooPerm_a is ordered. d_v[i] is the cooPerm_a[i]-th unique nonzero.
4338:       */
4339:       thrust::reduce_by_key(cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), cusp->cooPerm_a->end(), vbit, thrust::make_discard_iterator(), cooPerm_w->begin(), thrust::equal_to<PetscInt>(), thrust::plus<PetscScalar>());
4340:       thrust::transform(cooPerm_w->begin(), cooPerm_w->end(), matrix->values->begin(), matrix->values->begin(), thrust::plus<PetscScalar>());
4341:       delete cooPerm_w;
4342:     } else {
4343:       /* all nonzeros in d_v[] are unique entries */
4344:       auto zibit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(d_v, cusp->cooPerm->begin()), matrix->values->begin()));
4345:       auto zieit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(d_v, cusp->cooPerm->end()), matrix->values->end()));
4346:       thrust::for_each(zibit, zieit, VecCUDAPlusEquals()); /* values[i] += d_v[cooPerm[i]]  */
4347:     }
4348:   } else {
4349:     if (cusp->cooPerm_a) { /* repeated entries in COO, with INSERT_VALUES -> reduce */
4350:       auto vbit = thrust::make_permutation_iterator(d_v, cusp->cooPerm->begin());
4351:       thrust::reduce_by_key(cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), cusp->cooPerm_a->end(), vbit, thrust::make_discard_iterator(), matrix->values->begin(), thrust::equal_to<PetscInt>(), thrust::plus<PetscScalar>());
4352:     } else {
4353:       auto zibit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(d_v, cusp->cooPerm->begin()), matrix->values->begin()));
4354:       auto zieit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(d_v, cusp->cooPerm->end()), matrix->values->end()));
4355:       thrust::for_each(zibit, zieit, VecCUDAEquals());
4356:     }
4357:   }
4358:   PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
4359: finalize:
4360:   delete cooPerm_v;
4361:   A->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_GPU;
4362:   PetscCall(PetscObjectStateIncrease((PetscObject)A));
4363:   /* shorter version of MatAssemblyEnd_SeqAIJ */
4364:   PetscCall(PetscInfo(A, "Matrix size: %" PetscInt_FMT " X %" PetscInt_FMT "; storage space: 0 unneeded,%" PetscInt_FMT " used\n", A->rmap->n, A->cmap->n, a->nz));
4365:   PetscCall(PetscInfo(A, "Number of mallocs during MatSetValues() is 0\n"));
4366:   PetscCall(PetscInfo(A, "Maximum nonzeros in any row is %" PetscInt_FMT "\n", a->rmax));
4367:   a->reallocs = 0;
4368:   A->info.mallocs += 0;
4369:   A->info.nz_unneeded = 0;
4370:   A->assembled = A->was_assembled = PETSC_TRUE;
4371:   A->num_ass++;
4372:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4373: }

4375: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(Mat A, PetscBool destroy)
4376: {
4377:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;

4379:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4380:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4381:   if (!cusp) PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4382:   if (destroy) {
4383:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct_Destroy(&cusp->matTranspose, cusp->format));
4384:     delete cusp->csr2csc_i;
4385:     cusp->csr2csc_i = NULL;
4386:   }
4387:   A->transupdated = PETSC_FALSE;
4388:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4389: }

4391: #include <thrust/binary_search.h>
4392: /* 'Basic' means it only works when coo_i[] and coo_j[] do not contain negative indices */
4393: PetscErrorCode MatSetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE_Basic(Mat A, PetscCount n, PetscInt coo_i[], PetscInt coo_j[])
4394: {
4395:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4396:   Mat_SeqAIJ         *a    = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;
4397:   PetscInt            cooPerm_n, nzr = 0;

4399:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4400:   PetscCall(PetscLayoutSetUp(A->rmap));
4401:   PetscCall(PetscLayoutSetUp(A->cmap));
4402:   cooPerm_n = cusp->cooPerm ? cusp->cooPerm->size() : 0;
4403:   if (n != cooPerm_n) {
4404:     delete cusp->cooPerm;
4405:     delete cusp->cooPerm_a;
4406:     cusp->cooPerm   = NULL;
4407:     cusp->cooPerm_a = NULL;
4408:   }
4409:   if (n) {
4410:     thrust::device_ptr<PetscInt> d_i, d_j;
4411:     PetscInt                    *d_raw_i, *d_raw_j;
4412:     PetscBool                    free_raw_i = PETSC_FALSE, free_raw_j = PETSC_FALSE;
4413:     PetscMemType                 imtype, jmtype;

4415:     PetscCall(PetscGetMemType(coo_i, &imtype));
4416:     if (PetscMemTypeHost(imtype)) {
4417:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc(&d_raw_i, sizeof(PetscInt) * n));
4418:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(d_raw_i, coo_i, sizeof(PetscInt) * n, cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4419:       d_i        = thrust::device_pointer_cast(d_raw_i);
4420:       free_raw_i = PETSC_TRUE;
4421:       PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(1. * n * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4422:     } else {
4423:       d_i = thrust::device_pointer_cast(coo_i);
4424:     }

4426:     PetscCall(PetscGetMemType(coo_j, &jmtype));
4427:     if (PetscMemTypeHost(jmtype)) { // MatSetPreallocationCOO_MPIAIJCUSPARSE_Basic() passes device coo_i[] and host coo_j[]!
4428:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc(&d_raw_j, sizeof(PetscInt) * n));
4429:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(d_raw_j, coo_j, sizeof(PetscInt) * n, cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4430:       d_j        = thrust::device_pointer_cast(d_raw_j);
4431:       free_raw_j = PETSC_TRUE;
4432:       PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(1. * n * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4433:     } else {
4434:       d_j = thrust::device_pointer_cast(coo_j);
4435:     }

4437:     THRUSTINTARRAY ii(A->rmap->n);

4439:     if (!cusp->cooPerm) cusp->cooPerm = new THRUSTINTARRAY(n);
4440:     if (!cusp->cooPerm_a) cusp->cooPerm_a = new THRUSTINTARRAY(n);

4442:     /* Ex.
4443:       n = 6
4444:       coo_i = [3,3,1,4,1,4]
4445:       coo_j = [3,2,2,5,2,6]
4446:     */
4447:     auto fkey = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(d_i, d_j));
4448:     auto ekey = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(d_i + n, d_j + n));

4450:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
4451:     thrust::sequence(thrust::device, cusp->cooPerm->begin(), cusp->cooPerm->end(), 0);
4452:     thrust::sort_by_key(fkey, ekey, cusp->cooPerm->begin(), IJCompare()); /* sort by row, then by col */
4453:     (*cusp->cooPerm_a).assign(d_i, d_i + n);                              /* copy the sorted array */
4454:     THRUSTINTARRAY w(d_j, d_j + n);

4456:     /*
4457:       d_i     = [1,1,3,3,4,4]
4458:       d_j     = [2,2,2,3,5,6]
4459:       cooPerm = [2,4,1,0,3,5]
4460:     */
4461:     auto nekey = thrust::unique(fkey, ekey, IJEqual()); /* unique (d_i, d_j) */

4463:     /*
4464:       d_i     = [1,3,3,4,4,x]
4465:                             ^ekey
4466:       d_j     = [2,2,3,5,6,x]
4467:                            ^nekye
4468:     */
4469:     if (nekey == ekey) { /* all entries are unique */
4470:       delete cusp->cooPerm_a;
4471:       cusp->cooPerm_a = NULL;
4472:     } else { /* Stefano: I couldn't come up with a more elegant algorithm */
4473:       /* idea: any change in i or j in the (i,j) sequence implies a new nonzero */
4474:       adjacent_difference(cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), cusp->cooPerm_a->end(), cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), IJDiff()); /* cooPerm_a: [1,1,3,3,4,4] => [1,0,1,0,1,0]*/
4475:       adjacent_difference(w.begin(), w.end(), w.begin(), IJDiff());                                              /* w:         [2,2,2,3,5,6] => [2,0,0,1,1,1]*/
4476:       (*cusp->cooPerm_a)[0] = 0;                                                                                 /* clear the first entry, though accessing an entry on device implies a cudaMemcpy */
4477:       w[0]                  = 0;
4478:       thrust::transform(cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), cusp->cooPerm_a->end(), w.begin(), cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), IJSum());            /* cooPerm_a =          [0,0,1,1,1,1]*/
4479:       thrust::inclusive_scan(cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), cusp->cooPerm_a->end(), cusp->cooPerm_a->begin(), thrust::plus<PetscInt>()); /*cooPerm_a=[0,0,1,2,3,4]*/
4480:     }
4481:     thrust::counting_iterator<PetscInt> search_begin(0);
4482:     thrust::upper_bound(d_i, nekey.get_iterator_tuple().get<0>(), /* binary search entries of [0,1,2,3,4,5,6) in ordered array d_i = [1,3,3,4,4], supposing A->rmap->n = 6. */
4483:                         search_begin, search_begin + A->rmap->n,  /* return in ii[] the index of last position in d_i[] where value could be inserted without violating the ordering */
4484:                         ii.begin());                              /* ii = [0,1,1,3,5,5]. A leading 0 will be added later */
4485:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());

4487:     PetscCall(MatSeqXAIJFreeAIJ(A, &a->a, &a->j, &a->i));
4488:     a->singlemalloc = PETSC_FALSE;
4489:     a->free_a       = PETSC_TRUE;
4490:     a->free_ij      = PETSC_TRUE;
4491:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(A->rmap->n + 1, &a->i));
4492:     a->i[0] = 0; /* a->i = [0,0,1,1,3,5,5] */
4493:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(a->i + 1, ii.data().get(), A->rmap->n * sizeof(PetscInt), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4494:     a->nz = a->maxnz = a->i[A->rmap->n];
4495:     a->rmax          = 0;
4496:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(a->nz, &a->a));
4497:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(a->nz, &a->j));
4498:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(a->j, thrust::raw_pointer_cast(d_j), a->nz * sizeof(PetscInt), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4499:     if (!a->ilen) PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(A->rmap->n, &a->ilen));
4500:     if (!a->imax) PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(A->rmap->n, &a->imax));
4501:     for (PetscInt i = 0; i < A->rmap->n; i++) {
4502:       const PetscInt nnzr = a->i[i + 1] - a->i[i];
4503:       nzr += (PetscInt) !!(nnzr);
4504:       a->ilen[i] = a->imax[i] = nnzr;
4505:       a->rmax                 = PetscMax(a->rmax, nnzr);
4506:     }
4507:     a->nonzerorowcnt = nzr;
4508:     A->preallocated  = PETSC_TRUE;
4509:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuToCpu((A->rmap->n + a->nz) * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4510:     PetscCall(MatMarkDiagonal_SeqAIJ(A));
4511:     if (free_raw_i) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(d_raw_i));
4512:     if (free_raw_j) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree(d_raw_j));
4513:   } else {
4514:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJSetPreallocation(A, 0, NULL));
4515:   }
4516:   PetscCall(MatSetOption(A, MAT_NEW_NONZERO_ALLOCATION_ERR, PETSC_TRUE));

4518:   /* We want to allocate the CUSPARSE struct for matvec now.
4519:      The code is so convoluted now that I prefer to copy zeros */
4520:   PetscCall(PetscArrayzero(a->a, a->nz));
4521:   PetscCall(MatCheckCompressedRow(A, nzr, &a->compressedrow, a->i, A->rmap->n, 0.6));
4522:   A->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_CPU;
4523:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
4524:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(A, PETSC_TRUE));
4525:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4526: }

4528: PetscErrorCode MatSetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat mat, PetscCount coo_n, PetscInt coo_i[], PetscInt coo_j[])
4529: {
4530:   Mat_SeqAIJ         *seq;
4531:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *dev;
4532:   PetscBool           coo_basic = PETSC_TRUE;
4533:   PetscMemType        mtype     = PETSC_MEMTYPE_DEVICE;

4535:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4536:   PetscCall(MatResetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJ(mat));
4537:   PetscCall(MatResetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(mat));
4538:   if (coo_i) {
4539:     PetscCall(PetscGetMemType(coo_i, &mtype));
4540:     if (PetscMemTypeHost(mtype)) {
4541:       for (PetscCount k = 0; k < coo_n; k++) {
4542:         if (coo_i[k] < 0 || coo_j[k] < 0) {
4543:           coo_basic = PETSC_FALSE;
4544:           break;
4545:         }
4546:       }
4547:     }
4548:   }

4550:   if (coo_basic) { /* i,j are on device or do not contain negative indices */
4551:     PetscCall(MatSetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE_Basic(mat, coo_n, coo_i, coo_j));
4552:   } else {
4553:     PetscCall(MatSetPreallocationCOO_SeqAIJ(mat, coo_n, coo_i, coo_j));
4554:     mat->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_CPU;
4555:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(mat));
4556:     seq = static_cast<Mat_SeqAIJ *>(mat->data);
4557:     dev = static_cast<Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *>(mat->spptr);
4558:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&dev->jmap_d, (seq->nz + 1) * sizeof(PetscCount)));
4559:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(dev->jmap_d, seq->jmap, (seq->nz + 1) * sizeof(PetscCount), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4560:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&dev->perm_d, seq->Atot * sizeof(PetscCount)));
4561:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(dev->perm_d, seq->perm, seq->Atot * sizeof(PetscCount), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4562:     dev->use_extended_coo = PETSC_TRUE;
4563:   }
4564:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4565: }

4567: __global__ static void MatAddCOOValues(const PetscScalar kv[], PetscCount nnz, const PetscCount jmap[], const PetscCount perm[], InsertMode imode, PetscScalar a[])
4568: {
4569:   PetscCount       i         = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
4570:   const PetscCount grid_size = gridDim.x * blockDim.x;
4571:   for (; i < nnz; i += grid_size) {
4572:     PetscScalar sum = 0.0;
4573:     for (PetscCount k = jmap[i]; k < jmap[i + 1]; k++) sum += kv[perm[k]];
4574:     a[i] = (imode == INSERT_VALUES ? 0.0 : a[i]) + sum;
4575:   }
4576: }

4578: PetscErrorCode MatSetValuesCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, const PetscScalar v[], InsertMode imode)
4579: {
4580:   Mat_SeqAIJ         *seq  = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;
4581:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *dev  = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4582:   PetscCount          Annz = seq->nz;
4583:   PetscMemType        memtype;
4584:   const PetscScalar  *v1 = v;
4585:   PetscScalar        *Aa;

4587:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4588:   if (dev->use_extended_coo) {
4589:     PetscCall(PetscGetMemType(v, &memtype));
4590:     if (PetscMemTypeHost(memtype)) { /* If user gave v[] in host, we might need to copy it to device if any */
4591:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&v1, seq->coo_n * sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4592:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy((void *)v1, v, seq->coo_n * sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4593:     }

4595:     if (imode == INSERT_VALUES) PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite(A, &Aa));
4596:     else PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray(A, &Aa));

4598:     if (Annz) {
4599:       MatAddCOOValues<<<(Annz + 255) / 256, 256>>>(v1, Annz, dev->jmap_d, dev->perm_d, imode, Aa);
4600:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaPeekAtLastError());
4601:     }

4603:     if (imode == INSERT_VALUES) PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayWrite(A, &Aa));
4604:     else PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray(A, &Aa));

4606:     if (PetscMemTypeHost(memtype)) PetscCallCUDA(cudaFree((void *)v1));
4607:   } else {
4608:     PetscCall(MatSetValuesCOO_SeqAIJCUSPARSE_Basic(A, v, imode));
4609:   }
4610:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4611: }

4613: /*@C
4614:     MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetIJ - returns the device row storage `i` and `j` indices for `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrices.

4616:    Not Collective

4618:     Input Parameters:
4619: +   A - the matrix
4620: -   compressed - `PETSC_TRUE` or `PETSC_FALSE` indicating the matrix data structure should be always returned in compressed form

4622:     Output Parameters:
4623: +   i - the CSR row pointers
4624: -   j - the CSR column indices

4626:     Level: developer

4628:     Note:
4629:       When compressed is true, the CSR structure does not contain empty rows

4631: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreIJ()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead()`
4632: @*/
4633: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetIJ(Mat A, PetscBool compressed, const int **i, const int **j)
4634: {
4635:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4636:   CsrMatrix          *csr;
4637:   Mat_SeqAIJ         *a = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data;

4639:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4641:   if (!i || !j) PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4642:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4643:   PetscCheck(cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4644:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
4645:   PetscCheck(cusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
4646:   csr = (CsrMatrix *)cusp->mat->mat;
4647:   if (i) {
4648:     if (!compressed && a->compressedrow.use) { /* need full row offset */
4649:       if (!cusp->rowoffsets_gpu) {
4650:         cusp->rowoffsets_gpu = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(A->rmap->n + 1);
4651:         cusp->rowoffsets_gpu->assign(a->i, a->i + A->rmap->n + 1);
4652:         PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu((A->rmap->n + 1) * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4653:       }
4654:       *i = cusp->rowoffsets_gpu->data().get();
4655:     } else *i = csr->row_offsets->data().get();
4656:   }
4657:   if (j) *j = csr->column_indices->data().get();
4658:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4659: }

4661: /*@C
4662:     MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreIJ - restore the device row storage `i` and `j` indices obtained with `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetIJ()`

4664:    Not Collective

4666:     Input Parameters:
4667: +   A - the matrix
4668: .   compressed - `PETSC_TRUE` or `PETSC_FALSE` indicating the matrix data structure should be always returned in compressed form
4669: .   i - the CSR row pointers
4670: -   j - the CSR column indices

4672:     Level: developer

4674: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetIJ()`
4675: @*/
4676: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreIJ(Mat A, PetscBool compressed, const int **i, const int **j)
4677: {
4678:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4680:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4681:   if (i) *i = NULL;
4682:   if (j) *j = NULL;
4683:   (void)compressed;
4684:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4685: }

4687: /*@C
4688:    MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead - gives read-only access to the array where the device data for a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix is stored

4690:    Not Collective

4692:    Input Parameter:
4693: .   A - a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix

4695:    Output Parameter:
4696: .   a - pointer to the device data

4698:    Level: developer

4700:    Note:
4701:    May trigger host-device copies if up-to-date matrix data is on host

4703: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayRead()`
4704: @*/
4705: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead(Mat A, const PetscScalar **a)
4706: {
4707:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4708:   CsrMatrix          *csr;

4710:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4713:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4714:   PetscCheck(cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4715:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
4716:   PetscCheck(cusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
4717:   csr = (CsrMatrix *)cusp->mat->mat;
4718:   PetscCheck(csr->values, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing CUDA memory");
4719:   *a = csr->values->data().get();
4720:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4721: }

4723: /*@C
4724:    MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayRead - restore the read-only access array obtained from `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead()`

4726:    Not Collective

4728:    Input Parameters:
4729: +   A - a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix
4730: -   a - pointer to the device data

4732:    Level: developer

4734: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead()`
4735: @*/
4736: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayRead(Mat A, const PetscScalar **a)
4737: {
4738:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4741:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4742:   *a = NULL;
4743:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4744: }

4746: /*@C
4747:    MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray - gives read-write access to the array where the device data for a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix is stored

4749:    Not Collective

4751:    Input Parameter:
4752: .   A - a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix

4754:    Output Parameter:
4755: .   a - pointer to the device data

4757:    Level: developer

4759:    Note:
4760:    May trigger host-device copies if up-to-date matrix data is on host

4762: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray()`
4763: @*/
4764: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray(Mat A, PetscScalar **a)
4765: {
4766:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4767:   CsrMatrix          *csr;

4769:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4772:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4773:   PetscCheck(cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4774:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
4775:   PetscCheck(cusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
4776:   csr = (CsrMatrix *)cusp->mat->mat;
4777:   PetscCheck(csr->values, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing CUDA memory");
4778:   *a             = csr->values->data().get();
4779:   A->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_GPU;
4780:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(A, PETSC_FALSE));
4781:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4782: }
4783: /*@C
4784:    MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray - restore the read-write access array obtained from `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray()`

4786:    Not Collective

4788:    Input Parameters:
4789: +   A - a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix
4790: -   a - pointer to the device data

4792:    Level: developer

4794: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray()`
4795: @*/
4796: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArray(Mat A, PetscScalar **a)
4797: {
4798:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4801:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4802:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJInvalidateDiagonal(A));
4803:   PetscCall(PetscObjectStateIncrease((PetscObject)A));
4804:   *a = NULL;
4805:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4806: }

4808: /*@C
4809:    MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite - gives write access to the array where the device data for a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix is stored

4811:    Not Collective

4813:    Input Parameter:
4814: .   A - a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix

4816:    Output Parameter:
4817: .   a - pointer to the device data

4819:    Level: developer

4821:    Note:
4822:    Does not trigger host-device copies and flags data validity on the GPU

4824: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArray()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead()`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayWrite()`
4825: @*/
4826: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite(Mat A, PetscScalar **a)
4827: {
4828:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *cusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr;
4829:   CsrMatrix          *csr;

4831:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4834:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4835:   PetscCheck(cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && cusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4836:   PetscCheck(cusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
4837:   csr = (CsrMatrix *)cusp->mat->mat;
4838:   PetscCheck(csr->values, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing CUDA memory");
4839:   *a             = csr->values->data().get();
4840:   A->offloadmask = PETSC_OFFLOAD_GPU;
4841:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(A, PETSC_FALSE));
4842:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4843: }

4845: /*@C
4846:    MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayWrite - restore the write-only access array obtained from `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite()`

4848:    Not Collective

4850:    Input Parameters:
4851: +   A - a `MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE` matrix
4852: -   a - pointer to the device data

4854:    Level: developer

4856: .seealso: [](chapter_matrices), `Mat`, `MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayWrite()`
4857: @*/
4858: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayWrite(Mat A, PetscScalar **a)
4859: {
4860:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4863:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4864:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJInvalidateDiagonal(A));
4865:   PetscCall(PetscObjectStateIncrease((PetscObject)A));
4866:   *a = NULL;
4867:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4868: }

4870: struct IJCompare4 {
4871:   __host__ __device__ inline bool operator()(const thrust::tuple<int, int, PetscScalar, int> &t1, const thrust::tuple<int, int, PetscScalar, int> &t2)
4872:   {
4873:     if (t1.get<0>() < t2.get<0>()) return true;
4874:     if (t1.get<0>() == t2.get<0>()) return t1.get<1>() < t2.get<1>();
4875:     return false;
4876:   }
4877: };

4879: struct Shift {
4880:   int _shift;

4882:   Shift(int shift) : _shift(shift) { }
4883:   __host__ __device__ inline int operator()(const int &c) { return c + _shift; }
4884: };

4886: /* merges two SeqAIJCUSPARSE matrices A, B by concatenating their rows. [A';B']' operation in matlab notation */
4887: PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEMergeMats(Mat A, Mat B, MatReuse reuse, Mat *C)
4888: {
4889:   Mat_SeqAIJ                   *a = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)A->data, *b = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)B->data, *c;
4890:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE           *Acusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)A->spptr, *Bcusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)B->spptr, *Ccusp;
4891:   Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *Cmat;
4892:   CsrMatrix                    *Acsr, *Bcsr, *Ccsr;
4893:   PetscInt                      Annz, Bnnz;
4894:   cusparseStatus_t              stat;
4895:   PetscInt                      i, m, n, zero = 0;

4897:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4901:   PetscCheckTypeName(A, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4902:   PetscCheckTypeName(B, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE);
4903:   PetscCheck(A->rmap->n == B->rmap->n, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_ARG_SIZ, "Invalid number or rows %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, A->rmap->n, B->rmap->n);
4904:   PetscCheck(reuse != MAT_INPLACE_MATRIX, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "MAT_INPLACE_MATRIX not supported");
4905:   PetscCheck(Acusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && Acusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4906:   PetscCheck(Bcusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && Bcusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4907:   if (reuse == MAT_INITIAL_MATRIX) {
4908:     m = A->rmap->n;
4909:     n = A->cmap->n + B->cmap->n;
4910:     PetscCall(MatCreate(PETSC_COMM_SELF, C));
4911:     PetscCall(MatSetSizes(*C, m, n, m, n));
4912:     PetscCall(MatSetType(*C, MATSEQAIJCUSPARSE));
4913:     c                       = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)(*C)->data;
4914:     Ccusp                   = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)(*C)->spptr;
4915:     Cmat                    = new Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct;
4916:     Ccsr                    = new CsrMatrix;
4917:     Cmat->cprowIndices      = NULL;
4918:     c->compressedrow.use    = PETSC_FALSE;
4919:     c->compressedrow.nrows  = 0;
4920:     c->compressedrow.i      = NULL;
4921:     c->compressedrow.rindex = NULL;
4922:     Ccusp->workVector       = NULL;
4923:     Ccusp->nrows            = m;
4924:     Ccusp->mat              = Cmat;
4925:     Ccusp->mat->mat         = Ccsr;
4926:     Ccsr->num_rows          = m;
4927:     Ccsr->num_cols          = n;
4928:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseCreateMatDescr(&Cmat->descr));
4929:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetMatIndexBase(Cmat->descr, CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO));
4930:     PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetMatType(Cmat->descr, CUSPARSE_MATRIX_TYPE_GENERAL));
4931:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&(Cmat->alpha_one), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4932:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&(Cmat->beta_zero), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4933:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&(Cmat->beta_one), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4934:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(Cmat->alpha_one, &PETSC_CUSPARSE_ONE, sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4935:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(Cmat->beta_zero, &PETSC_CUSPARSE_ZERO, sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4936:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(Cmat->beta_one, &PETSC_CUSPARSE_ONE, sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
4937:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
4938:     PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(B));
4939:     PetscCheck(Acusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
4940:     PetscCheck(Bcusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");

4942:     Acsr                 = (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->mat->mat;
4943:     Bcsr                 = (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->mat->mat;
4944:     Annz                 = (PetscInt)Acsr->column_indices->size();
4945:     Bnnz                 = (PetscInt)Bcsr->column_indices->size();
4946:     c->nz                = Annz + Bnnz;
4947:     Ccsr->row_offsets    = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(m + 1);
4948:     Ccsr->column_indices = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(c->nz);
4949:     Ccsr->values         = new THRUSTARRAY(c->nz);
4950:     Ccsr->num_entries    = c->nz;
4951:     Ccusp->cooPerm       = new THRUSTINTARRAY(c->nz);
4952:     if (c->nz) {
4953:       auto              Acoo = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(Annz);
4954:       auto              Bcoo = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(Bnnz);
4955:       auto              Ccoo = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(c->nz);
4956:       THRUSTINTARRAY32 *Aroff, *Broff;

4958:       if (a->compressedrow.use) { /* need full row offset */
4959:         if (!Acusp->rowoffsets_gpu) {
4960:           Acusp->rowoffsets_gpu = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(A->rmap->n + 1);
4961:           Acusp->rowoffsets_gpu->assign(a->i, a->i + A->rmap->n + 1);
4962:           PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu((A->rmap->n + 1) * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4963:         }
4964:         Aroff = Acusp->rowoffsets_gpu;
4965:       } else Aroff = Acsr->row_offsets;
4966:       if (b->compressedrow.use) { /* need full row offset */
4967:         if (!Bcusp->rowoffsets_gpu) {
4968:           Bcusp->rowoffsets_gpu = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(B->rmap->n + 1);
4969:           Bcusp->rowoffsets_gpu->assign(b->i, b->i + B->rmap->n + 1);
4970:           PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu((B->rmap->n + 1) * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4971:         }
4972:         Broff = Bcusp->rowoffsets_gpu;
4973:       } else Broff = Bcsr->row_offsets;
4974:       PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
4975:       stat = cusparseXcsr2coo(Acusp->handle, Aroff->data().get(), Annz, m, Acoo->data().get(), CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO);
4976:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(stat);
4977:       stat = cusparseXcsr2coo(Bcusp->handle, Broff->data().get(), Bnnz, m, Bcoo->data().get(), CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO);
4978:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(stat);
4979:       /* Issues when using bool with large matrices on SUMMIT 10.2.89 */
4980:       auto Aperm = thrust::make_constant_iterator(1);
4981:       auto Bperm = thrust::make_constant_iterator(0);
4982: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(10, 0, 0)
4983:       auto Bcib = thrust::make_transform_iterator(Bcsr->column_indices->begin(), Shift(A->cmap->n));
4984:       auto Bcie = thrust::make_transform_iterator(Bcsr->column_indices->end(), Shift(A->cmap->n));
4985: #else
4986:       /* there are issues instantiating the merge operation using a transform iterator for the columns of B */
4987:       auto Bcib = Bcsr->column_indices->begin();
4988:       auto Bcie = Bcsr->column_indices->end();
4989:       thrust::transform(Bcib, Bcie, Bcib, Shift(A->cmap->n));
4990: #endif
4991:       auto wPerm = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(Annz + Bnnz);
4992:       auto Azb   = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Acoo->begin(), Acsr->column_indices->begin(), Acsr->values->begin(), Aperm));
4993:       auto Aze   = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Acoo->end(), Acsr->column_indices->end(), Acsr->values->end(), Aperm));
4994:       auto Bzb   = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Bcoo->begin(), Bcib, Bcsr->values->begin(), Bperm));
4995:       auto Bze   = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Bcoo->end(), Bcie, Bcsr->values->end(), Bperm));
4996:       auto Czb   = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Ccoo->begin(), Ccsr->column_indices->begin(), Ccsr->values->begin(), wPerm->begin()));
4997:       auto p1    = Ccusp->cooPerm->begin();
4998:       auto p2    = Ccusp->cooPerm->begin();
4999:       thrust::advance(p2, Annz);
5000:       PetscCallThrust(thrust::merge(thrust::device, Azb, Aze, Bzb, Bze, Czb, IJCompare4()));
5001: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_LT(10, 0, 0)
5002:       thrust::transform(Bcib, Bcie, Bcib, Shift(-A->cmap->n));
5003: #endif
5004:       auto cci = thrust::make_counting_iterator(zero);
5005:       auto cce = thrust::make_counting_iterator(c->nz);
5006: #if 0 //Errors on SUMMIT cuda 11.1.0
5007:       PetscCallThrust(thrust::partition_copy(thrust::device,cci,cce,wPerm->begin(),p1,p2,thrust::identity<int>()));
5008: #else
5009:       auto pred = thrust::identity<int>();
5010:       PetscCallThrust(thrust::copy_if(thrust::device, cci, cce, wPerm->begin(), p1, pred));
5011:       PetscCallThrust(thrust::remove_copy_if(thrust::device, cci, cce, wPerm->begin(), p2, pred));
5012: #endif
5013:       stat = cusparseXcoo2csr(Ccusp->handle, Ccoo->data().get(), c->nz, m, Ccsr->row_offsets->data().get(), CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO);
5014:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(stat);
5015:       PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
5016:       delete wPerm;
5017:       delete Acoo;
5018:       delete Bcoo;
5019:       delete Ccoo;
5020: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
5021:       stat = cusparseCreateCsr(&Cmat->matDescr, Ccsr->num_rows, Ccsr->num_cols, Ccsr->num_entries, Ccsr->row_offsets->data().get(), Ccsr->column_indices->data().get(), Ccsr->values->data().get(), CUSPARSE_INDEX_32I, CUSPARSE_INDEX_32I, CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO, cusparse_scalartype);
5022:       PetscCallCUSPARSE(stat);
5023: #endif
5024:       if (A->form_explicit_transpose && B->form_explicit_transpose) { /* if A and B have the transpose, generate C transpose too */
5025:         PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEFormExplicitTranspose(A));
5026:         PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEFormExplicitTranspose(B));
5027:         PetscBool                     AT = Acusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE, BT = Bcusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
5028:         Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct *CmatT = new Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct;
5029:         CsrMatrix                    *CcsrT = new CsrMatrix;
5030:         CsrMatrix                    *AcsrT = AT ? (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;
5031:         CsrMatrix                    *BcsrT = BT ? (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;

5033:         (*C)->form_explicit_transpose = PETSC_TRUE;
5034:         (*C)->transupdated            = PETSC_TRUE;
5035:         Ccusp->rowoffsets_gpu         = NULL;
5036:         CmatT->cprowIndices           = NULL;
5037:         CmatT->mat                    = CcsrT;
5038:         CcsrT->num_rows               = n;
5039:         CcsrT->num_cols               = m;
5040:         CcsrT->num_entries            = c->nz;

5042:         CcsrT->row_offsets    = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(n + 1);
5043:         CcsrT->column_indices = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(c->nz);
5044:         CcsrT->values         = new THRUSTARRAY(c->nz);

5046:         PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
5047:         auto rT = CcsrT->row_offsets->begin();
5048:         if (AT) {
5049:           rT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->row_offsets->begin(), AcsrT->row_offsets->end(), rT);
5050:           thrust::advance(rT, -1);
5051:         }
5052:         if (BT) {
5053:           auto titb = thrust::make_transform_iterator(BcsrT->row_offsets->begin(), Shift(a->nz));
5054:           auto tite = thrust::make_transform_iterator(BcsrT->row_offsets->end(), Shift(a->nz));
5055:           thrust::copy(titb, tite, rT);
5056:         }
5057:         auto cT = CcsrT->column_indices->begin();
5058:         if (AT) cT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->column_indices->begin(), AcsrT->column_indices->end(), cT);
5059:         if (BT) thrust::copy(BcsrT->column_indices->begin(), BcsrT->column_indices->end(), cT);
5060:         auto vT = CcsrT->values->begin();
5061:         if (AT) vT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->values->begin(), AcsrT->values->end(), vT);
5062:         if (BT) thrust::copy(BcsrT->values->begin(), BcsrT->values->end(), vT);
5063:         PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());

5065:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseCreateMatDescr(&CmatT->descr));
5066:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetMatIndexBase(CmatT->descr, CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO));
5067:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(cusparseSetMatType(CmatT->descr, CUSPARSE_MATRIX_TYPE_GENERAL));
5068:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&(CmatT->alpha_one), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
5069:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&(CmatT->beta_zero), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
5070:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMalloc((void **)&(CmatT->beta_one), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
5071:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(CmatT->alpha_one, &PETSC_CUSPARSE_ONE, sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
5072:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(CmatT->beta_zero, &PETSC_CUSPARSE_ZERO, sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
5073:         PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(CmatT->beta_one, &PETSC_CUSPARSE_ONE, sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice));
5074: #if PETSC_PKG_CUDA_VERSION_GE(11, 0, 0)
5075:         stat = cusparseCreateCsr(&CmatT->matDescr, CcsrT->num_rows, CcsrT->num_cols, CcsrT->num_entries, CcsrT->row_offsets->data().get(), CcsrT->column_indices->data().get(), CcsrT->values->data().get(), CUSPARSE_INDEX_32I, CUSPARSE_INDEX_32I, CUSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO, cusparse_scalartype);
5076:         PetscCallCUSPARSE(stat);
5077: #endif
5078:         Ccusp->matTranspose = CmatT;
5079:       }
5080:     }

5082:     c->singlemalloc = PETSC_FALSE;
5083:     c->free_a       = PETSC_TRUE;
5084:     c->free_ij      = PETSC_TRUE;
5085:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(m + 1, &c->i));
5086:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(c->nz, &c->j));
5087:     if (PetscDefined(USE_64BIT_INDICES)) { /* 32 to 64 bit conversion on the GPU and then copy to host (lazy) */
5088:       THRUSTINTARRAY ii(Ccsr->row_offsets->size());
5089:       THRUSTINTARRAY jj(Ccsr->column_indices->size());
5090:       ii = *Ccsr->row_offsets;
5091:       jj = *Ccsr->column_indices;
5092:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(c->i, ii.data().get(), Ccsr->row_offsets->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
5093:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(c->j, jj.data().get(), Ccsr->column_indices->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
5094:     } else {
5095:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(c->i, Ccsr->row_offsets->data().get(), Ccsr->row_offsets->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
5096:       PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(c->j, Ccsr->column_indices->data().get(), Ccsr->column_indices->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
5097:     }
5098:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuToCpu((Ccsr->column_indices->size() + Ccsr->row_offsets->size()) * sizeof(PetscInt)));
5099:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(m, &c->ilen));
5100:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(m, &c->imax));
5101:     c->maxnz         = c->nz;
5102:     c->nonzerorowcnt = 0;
5103:     c->rmax          = 0;
5104:     for (i = 0; i < m; i++) {
5105:       const PetscInt nn = c->i[i + 1] - c->i[i];
5106:       c->ilen[i] = c->imax[i] = nn;
5107:       c->nonzerorowcnt += (PetscInt) !!nn;
5108:       c->rmax = PetscMax(c->rmax, nn);
5109:     }
5110:     PetscCall(MatMarkDiagonal_SeqAIJ(*C));
5111:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(c->nz, &c->a));
5112:     (*C)->nonzerostate++;
5113:     PetscCall(PetscLayoutSetUp((*C)->rmap));
5114:     PetscCall(PetscLayoutSetUp((*C)->cmap));
5115:     Ccusp->nonzerostate = (*C)->nonzerostate;
5116:     (*C)->preallocated  = PETSC_TRUE;
5117:   } else {
5118:     PetscCheck((*C)->rmap->n == B->rmap->n, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_ARG_SIZ, "Invalid number or rows %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, (*C)->rmap->n, B->rmap->n);
5119:     c = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)(*C)->data;
5120:     if (c->nz) {
5121:       Ccusp = (Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSE *)(*C)->spptr;
5122:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->cooPerm, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing cooPerm");
5123:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_ELL && Ccusp->format != MAT_CUSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
5124:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->nonzerostate == (*C)->nonzerostate, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Wrong nonzerostate");
5125:       PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
5126:       PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSECopyToGPU(B));
5127:       PetscCheck(Acusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
5128:       PetscCheck(Bcusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
5129:       Acsr = (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->mat->mat;
5130:       Bcsr = (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->mat->mat;
5131:       Ccsr = (CsrMatrix *)Ccusp->mat->mat;
5132:       PetscCheck(Acsr->num_entries == (PetscInt)Acsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "A nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, Acsr->num_entries, (PetscInt)Acsr->values->size());
5133:       PetscCheck(Bcsr->num_entries == (PetscInt)Bcsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "B nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, Bcsr->num_entries, (PetscInt)Bcsr->values->size());
5134:       PetscCheck(Ccsr->num_entries == (PetscInt)Ccsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "C nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, Ccsr->num_entries, (PetscInt)Ccsr->values->size());
5135:       PetscCheck(Ccsr->num_entries == Acsr->num_entries + Bcsr->num_entries, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "C nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT " + %" PetscInt_FMT, Ccsr->num_entries, Acsr->num_entries, Bcsr->num_entries);
5136:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->cooPerm->size() == Ccsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "permSize %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, (PetscInt)Ccusp->cooPerm->size(), (PetscInt)Ccsr->values->size());
5137:       auto pmid = Ccusp->cooPerm->begin();
5138:       thrust::advance(pmid, Acsr->num_entries);
5139:       PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
5140:       auto zibait = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Acsr->values->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), Ccusp->cooPerm->begin())));
5141:       auto zieait = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Acsr->values->end(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), pmid)));
5142:       thrust::for_each(zibait, zieait, VecCUDAEquals());
5143:       auto zibbit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Bcsr->values->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), pmid)));
5144:       auto ziebit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Bcsr->values->end(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), Ccusp->cooPerm->end())));
5145:       thrust::for_each(zibbit, ziebit, VecCUDAEquals());
5146:       PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(*C, PETSC_FALSE));
5147:       if (A->form_explicit_transpose && B->form_explicit_transpose && (*C)->form_explicit_transpose) {
5148:         PetscCheck(Ccusp->matTranspose, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing transpose Mat_SeqAIJCUSPARSEMultStruct");
5149:         PetscBool  AT = Acusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE, BT = Bcusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
5150:         CsrMatrix *AcsrT = AT ? (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;
5151:         CsrMatrix *BcsrT = BT ? (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;
5152:         CsrMatrix *CcsrT = (CsrMatrix *)Ccusp->matTranspose->mat;
5153:         auto       vT    = CcsrT->values->begin();
5154:         if (AT) vT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->values->begin(), AcsrT->values->end(), vT);
5155:         if (BT) thrust::copy(BcsrT->values->begin(), BcsrT->values->end(), vT);
5156:         (*C)->transupdated = PETSC_TRUE;
5157:       }
5158:       PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
5159:     }
5160:   }
5161:   PetscCall(PetscObjectStateIncrease((PetscObject)*C));
5162:   (*C)->assembled     = PETSC_TRUE;
5163:   (*C)->was_assembled = PETSC_FALSE;
5164:   (*C)->offloadmask   = PETSC_OFFLOAD_GPU;
5165:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
5166: }

5168: static PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCopySubArray_SeqAIJCUSPARSE(Mat A, PetscInt n, const PetscInt idx[], PetscScalar v[])
5169: {
5170:   bool               dmem;
5171:   const PetscScalar *av;

5173:   PetscFunctionBegin;
5174:   dmem = isCudaMem(v);
5175:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSEGetArrayRead(A, &av));
5176:   if (n && idx) {
5177:     THRUSTINTARRAY widx(n);
5178:     widx.assign(idx, idx + n);
5179:     PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(n * sizeof(PetscInt)));

5181:     THRUSTARRAY                    *w = NULL;
5182:     thrust::device_ptr<PetscScalar> dv;
5183:     if (dmem) {
5184:       dv = thrust::device_pointer_cast(v);
5185:     } else {
5186:       w  = new THRUSTARRAY(n);
5187:       dv = w->data();
5188:     }
5189:     thrust::device_ptr<const PetscScalar> dav = thrust::device_pointer_cast(av);

5191:     auto zibit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(dav, widx.begin()), dv));
5192:     auto zieit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(dav, widx.end()), dv + n));
5193:     thrust::for_each(zibit, zieit, VecCUDAEquals());
5194:     if (w) PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(v, w->data().get(), n * sizeof(PetscScalar), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
5195:     delete w;
5196:   } else {
5197:     PetscCallCUDA(cudaMemcpy(v, av, n * sizeof(PetscScalar), dmem ? cudaMemcpyDeviceToDevice : cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost));
5198:   }
5199:   if (!dmem) PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(n * sizeof(PetscScalar)));
5200:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJCUSPARSERestoreArrayRead(A, &av));
5201:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
5202: }
